Check component types exist in registry\n    for (const comp of exp.components) {\n      if (!REGISTERED_TYPES.has(comp.type)) {\n        issues.push({ id: exp.id, severity: 'P0', issue: 'Component type \\\"' + comp.type + '\\\" NOT in registry' });\n      }\n    }\n    \n    // 2. Check pinAssignments exist\n    if (!exp.pinAssignments || Object.keys(exp.pinAssignments).length === 0) {\n      issues.push({ id: exp.id, severity: 'P0', issue: 'MISSING pinAssignments (empty or undefined)' });\n    }\n    \n    // 3. Check connections exist\n    if (!exp.connections || exp.connections.length === 0) {\n      issues.push({ id: exp.id, severity: 'P0', issue: 'MISSING connections' });\n    }\n    \n    // 4. Check buildSteps exist\n    if (!exp.buildSteps || exp.buildSteps.length === 0) {\n      issues.push({ id: exp.id, severity: 'P1', issue: 'MISSING buildSteps (Passo Passo)' });\n    }\n    \n    // 5. Check layout exists for all components\n    if (exp.layout) {\n      for (const comp of exp.components) {\n        if (!exp.layout[comp.id]) {\n          issues.push({ id: exp.id, severity: 'P1', issue: 'Layout missing for component: ' + comp.id });\n        }\n      }\n    } else {\n      issues.push({ id: exp.id, severity: 'P1', issue: 'MISSING layout object' });\n    }\n    \n    // 6. Check quiz exists\n    if (!exp.quiz || exp.quiz.length === 0) {\n      issues.push({ id: exp.id, severity: 'P2', issue: 'MISSING quiz' });\n    }\n    \n    // 7. Check steps (text instructions) exist\n    if (!exp.steps || exp.steps.length === 0) {\n      issues.push({ id: exp.id, severity: 'P2', issue: 'MISSING steps (text instructions)' });\n    }\n    \n    // 8.
